# 登录

API:

https://psync.48.cn/syncsystem/api/cache/v1/update/overview

打开口袋48后的相关缓存数据

## 请求头：
```python
{
    "Host": "psync.48.cn",
    "version": "5.0.1",
    "os": "android",
    "Accept-Encoding": "gzip",
    "IMEI": "866716037125810",
    "User-Agent": "Mobile_Pocket",
    "Content-Length": "444",
    "Connection": "Keep-Alive",
    "Content-Type": "application/json;charset=utf-8",
    "token": "0"
}
```

## 表单数据：
```python
{
    "videoTypeUtime": "2017-03-24 15:59:11",
    "musicAlbumUtime": "2017-04-18 14:45:37",
    "functionUtime": "2017-05-17 16:28:26",
    "groupUtime": "2016-11-01 00:00:00",
    "memberInfoUtime": "2017-05-19 15:30:00",
    "talkUtime": "2017-05-05 18:04:52",
    "videoUtime": "2017-05-17 18:36:32",
    "musicUtime": "2017-05-05 15:56:11",
    "urlUtime": "2017-05-18 15:53:37",
    "teamUtime": "2017-04-26 18:15:37",
    "memberPropertyUtime": "2017-02-20 18:57:48",
    "periodUtime": "2017-04-29 15:47:00"
}
```
